English: <s>2004 Olympic silver medallist Amir Khan said, "Deep down I think women shouldn’t fight. That’s my opinion."</s>

English: <s>This is something you always need to keep in mind, to avoid disappointment or perhaps even distaste over local ways to do things.</s>

English: <s>The pit is either heated with hot stones from a fire, or in some places geothermal heat makes areas of ground naturally hot.</s>
